                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = aristocratic_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = populist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = traditionalist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = {
					value = 10000
					desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
				}
			}
		} 
	} 
	salary = { round = no gold = medium_court_position_salary } 
	scaling_employer_modifiers = { 
		terrible = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.1 } 
		poor = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.2 } 
		average = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.3 } 
		good = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.4 } 
		excellent = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.5 } 
	} 
	modifier = { monthly_prestige = minor_court_position_prestige_salary } 
	on_court_position_received = { 
		if = {
			limit = {scope:employee = { is_landed = no } }
			scope:liege = { save_scope_as = employer_saved } 
			scope:employee = { save_scope_as = employee_saved } 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { type = granted save_scope_as = title_change add_claim_on_loss = no } 
			title:k_orientis = { change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } 
			title:k_orientis = { random_in_de_facto_hierarchy = { limit = { tier = tier_county holder.highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy OR = { holder = { has_title = title:k_orientis } holder = { highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom } } } change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } holder = { random_vassal = { limit = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_county } change_liege = { liege = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { 
				type = swear_fealty 
				save_scope_as = title_change_2 add_claim_on_loss = no 
			} 
			scope:employee_saved = { change_liege = { liege = scope:employer_saved change = scope:title_change_2 } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change_2 
			change_government = imperial_government
		}
	} 
	on_court_position_revoked = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes k_orientis_revoked_effect = yes } 
	on_court_position_invalidated = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes }
	candidate_score = { 
		value = 250 
		add = scope:base_value 
		add = court_position_candidate_score_base_value 
		 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = scope:firing_court_position }
				scope:employee = { has_any_court_position = yes }
			}
			add = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = aristocratic_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = populist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = traditionalist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
				}
				}
			}
			add = {
				value = 10000
				desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
					has_title = title:k_orientis
				}
			}
			add = 200 #to stop AI from revoking alot 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:liege = {
					has_relation_rival = scope:employee
				}
			}
			add = 900 # rival isn't that big of a deal
		}
	} 
}
k_nikaea_governor = { 
	skill = stewardship max_available_positions = 1 
	category = court_position_roman_vicar 
	opinion = { value = regular_court_position_opinion } 
	aptitude_level_breakpoints = { 20 40 60 80 } 
	aptitude = { value = 25 add = { value = stewardship multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_stewardship } add = { value = martial multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_martial } if = { limit = { has_trait = administrator } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_administrator_trait } } if = { limit = { has_trait = overseer } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_overseer_trait } } } 
	is_shown = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				has_title = title:k_nikaea
			}
			AND = {
			has_title = title:k_nikaea
			NOT = { capital_county.kingdom = title:k_nikaea  }
			}
		}
	} 
	valid_position = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
	} 

	valid_character = { 
		scope:employee = { 
			OR = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							exists = title:k_nikaea.holder
						
							NOT = { scope:liege = title:k_nikaea.holder }
							
						}
						title:k_nikaea.holder = {
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = aristocratic_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = populist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = traditionalist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						liege = {
							has_title = title:k_nikaea
						}
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				has_title = title:k_nikaea
				
			}
		} 
	} 
	revoke_cost = { 
		prestige = {
			value = 1000
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = title:k_nikaea.holder
					title:k_nikaea.holder = {
						OR = {
							AND = {

                                    }

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = aristocratic_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = populist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = traditionalist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = {
					value = 10000
					desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
				}
			}
		} 
	} 
	salary = { round = no gold = medium_court_position_salary } 
	scaling_employer_modifiers = { 
		terrible = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.1 } 
		poor = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.2 } 
		average = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.3 } 
		good = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.4 } 
		excellent = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.5 } 
	} 
	modifier = { monthly_prestige = minor_court_position_prestige_salary } 
	on_court_position_received = { 
		if = {
			limit = {scope:employee = { is_landed = no } }
			scope:liege = { save_scope_as = employer_saved } 
			scope:employee = { save_scope_as = employee_saved } 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { type = granted save_scope_as = title_change add_claim_on_loss = no } 
			title:k_nikaea = { change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } }

			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { 
				type = swear_fealty 
				save_scope_as = title_change_2 add_claim_on_loss = no 
			} 
			scope:employee_saved = { change_liege = { liege = scope:employer_saved change = scope:title_change_2 } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change_2

	}

	on_court_position_invalidated = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes }

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern

	skill = stewardship max_available_positions = 1 
	category = court_position_roman_vicar 
	opinion = { value = regular_court_position_opinion } 
	aptitude_level_breakpoints = { 20 40 60 80 } 
	aptitude = { value = 25 add = { value = stewardship multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_stewardship } add = { value = martial multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_martial } if = { limit = { has_trait = administrator } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_administrator_trait } } if = { limit = { has_trait = overseer } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_overseer_trait } } } 
	is_shown = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				has_title = title:k_macedoniae
			}
			AND = {
			has_title = title:k_macedoniae
			NOT = { capital_county.kingdom = title:k_macedoniae  }
			}
		}

		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
	} 

	valid_character = { 
		scope:employee = { 
			OR = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							exists = title:k_macedoniae.holder
						
							NOT = { scope:liege = title:k_macedoniae.holder }
							
						}
						title:k_macedoniae.holder = {
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = aristocratic_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = populist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = traditionalist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						liege = {
							has_title = title:k_macedoniae
						}
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				has_title = title:k_macedoniae
				
			}
		} 
	} 
	revoke_cost = { 
		prestige = {
			value = 1000
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = title:k_macedoniae.holder
					title:k_macedoniae.holder = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = aristocratic_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = populist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = traditionalist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}

								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {

								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = {
					value = 10000
					desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
				}
			}
		} 
	} 
	salary = { round = no gold = medium_court_position_salary } 
	scaling_employer_modifiers = { 
		terrible = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.1 } 
		poor = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.2 } 
		average = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.3 } 
		good = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.4 } 
		excellent = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.5 } 
	} 
	modifier = { monthly_prestige = minor_court_position_prestige_salary } 
	on_court_position_received = { 
		if = {
			limit = {scope:employee = { is_landed = no } }
			scope:liege = { save_scope_as = employer_saved } 
			scope:employee = { save_scope_as = employee_saved } 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { type = granted save_scope_as = title_change add_claim_on_loss = no } 
			title:k_macedoniae = { change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } 
			title:k_macedoniae = { random_in_de_facto_hierarchy = { limit = { tier = tier_county holder.highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy OR = { holder = { has_title = title:k_macedoniae } holder = { highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom } } } change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } holder = { random_vassal = { limit = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_county } change_liege = { liege = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { 
				type = swear_fealty 
				save_scope_as = title_change_2 add_claim_on_loss = no 
			} 
			scope:employee_saved = { change_liege = { liege = scope:employer_saved change = scope:title_change_2 } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change_2 
			change_government = imperial_government
		}
	} 
	on_court_position_revoked = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes k_macedoniae_revoked_effect = yes } 
	on_court_position_invalidated = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes }
	candidate_score = { 
		value = 250 
		add = scope:base_value 
		add = court_position_candidate_score_base_value 
		 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = scope:firing_court_position }
				scope:employee = { has_any_court_position = yes }
			}
			add = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = aristocratic_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = populist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = traditionalist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
				}
				}
			}
			add = {
				value = 10000
				desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
					has_title = title:k_macedoniae
				}
			}
			add = 200 #to stop AI from revoking alot 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:liege = {
					has_relation_rival = scope:employee
				}
			}
			add = 900 # rival isn't that big of a deal
		}
	} 
}
k_saruhan_governor = { 
	skill = stewardship max_available_positions = 1 
	category = court_position_roman_vicar 
	opinion = { value = regular_court_position_opinion } 
	aptitude_level_breakpoints = { 20 40 60 80 } 
	aptitude = { value = 25 add = { value = stewardship multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_stewardship } add = { value = martial multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_martial } if = { limit = { has_trait = administrator } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_administrator_trait } } if = { limit = { has_trait = overseer } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_overseer_trait } } } 
	is_shown = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				has_title = title:k_saruhan
			}
			AND = {
			has_title = title:k_saruhan
			NOT = { capital_county.kingdom = title:k_saruhan  }
			}
		}
	} 
	valid_position = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
	} 

	valid_character = { 
		scope:employee = { 
			OR = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							exists = title:k_saruhan.holder
						
							NOT = { scope:liege = title:k_saruhan.holder }
							
						}
						title:k_saruhan.holder = {
							NOT = {

                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }

                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = aristocratic_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {

										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

						has_trait = high_senator

                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = aristocratic_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = populist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = traditionalist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
				}
				}
			}
			add = {
				value = 10000
				desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
					has_title = title:k_saruhan
				}
			}
			add = 200 #to stop AI from revoking alot 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:liege = {
					has_relation_rival = scope:employee
				}
			}
			add = 900 # rival isn't that big of a deal
		}
	} 
}
k_trinacria_governor = { 
	skill = stewardship max_available_positions = 1 
	category = court_position_roman_vicar 
	opinion = { value = regular_court_position_opinion } 
	aptitude_level_breakpoints = { 20 40 60 80 } 
	aptitude = { value = 25 add = { value = stewardship multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_stewardship } add = { value = martial multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_martial } if = { limit = { has_trait = administrator } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_administrator_trait } } if = { limit = { has_trait = overseer } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_overseer_trait } } } 
	is_shown = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				has_title = title:k_trinacria
			}
			AND = {
			has_title = title:k_trinacria
			NOT = { capital_county.kingdom = title:k_trinacria  }
			}
		}
	} 
	valid_position = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
	} 

	valid_character = { 
		scope:employee = { 
			OR = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							exists = title:k_trinacria.holder
						
							NOT = { scope:liege = title:k_trinacria.holder }
							
						}
						title:k_trinacria.holder = {
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = aristocratic_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = populist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = traditionalist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						liege = {
							has_title = title:k_trinacria
						}
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				has_title = title:k_trinacria
				
			}
		} 
	} 
	revoke_cost = { 
		prestige = {
			value = 1000
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = title:k_trinacria.holder
					title:k_trinacria.holder = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = aristocratic_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = populist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = traditionalist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = {
					value = 10000
					desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
				}
			}
		} 
	} 
	salary = { round = no gold = medium_court_position_salary } 
	scaling_employer_modifiers = { 
		terrible = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.1 } 
		poor = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.2 } 
		average = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.3 } 
		good = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.4 } 
		excellent = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.5 } 
	} 
	modifier = { monthly_prestige = minor_court_position_prestige_salary } 
	on_court_position_received = { 
		if = {
		limit = {scope:employee = { is_landed = no } }
			scope:liege = { save_scope_as = employer_saved } 
			scope:employee = { save_scope_as = employee_saved } 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { type = granted save_scope_as = title_change add_claim_on_loss = no } 
			title:k_trinacria = { change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } 
			title:k_trinacria = { random_in_de_facto_hierarchy = { limit = { tier = tier_county holder.highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy OR = { holder = { has_title = title:k_trinacria } holder = { highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom } } } change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } holder = { random_vassal = { limit = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_county } change_liege = { liege = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { 
				type = swear_fealty 
				save_scope_as = title_change_2 add_claim_on_loss = no 
			} 
			scope:employee_saved = { change_liege = { liege = scope:employer_saved change = scope:title_change_2 } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change_2 
			change_government = imperial_government
		}
	} 
	on_court_position_revoked = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes k_trinacria_revoked_effect = yes } 
	on_court_position_invalidated = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes }
	candidate_score = { 
		value = 250 
		add = scope:base_value 
		add = court_position_candidate_score_base_value 
		 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = scope:firing_court_position }
				scope:employee = { has_any_court_position = yes }
			}
			add = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = aristocratic_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = populist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = traditionalist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy

                                    }
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = aristocratic_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = populist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = traditionalist_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = {
					value = 10000
					desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
				}
			}
		} 
	} 
	salary = { round = no gold = medium_court_position_salary } 
	scaling_employer_modifiers = { 
		terrible = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.1 } 
		poor = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.2 } 
		average = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.3 } 
		good = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.4 } 
		excellent = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.5 } 
	} 
	modifier = { monthly_prestige = minor_court_position_prestige_salary } 
	on_court_position_received = { 
		if = {
		limit = {scope:employee = { is_landed = no } }
			scope:liege = { save_scope_as = employer_saved } 
			scope:employee = { save_scope_as = employee_saved } 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { type = granted save_scope_as = title_change add_claim_on_loss = no } 
			title:k_tekke = { change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } 
			title:k_tekke = { random_in_de_facto_hierarchy = { limit = { tier = tier_county holder.highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy OR = { holder = { has_title = title:k_tekke } holder = { highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom } } } change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } holder = { random_vassal = { limit = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_county } change_liege = { liege = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { 
				type = swear_fealty 
				save_scope_as = title_change_2 add_claim_on_loss = no 
			} 
			scope:employee_saved = { change_liege = { liege = scope:employer_saved change = scope:title_change_2 } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change_2 
			change_government = imperial_government
		}
	} 
	on_court_position_revoked = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes k_tekke_revoked_effect = yes } 
	on_court_position_invalidated = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes }
	candidate_score = { 
		value = 250 
		add = scope:base_value 
		add = court_position_candidate_score_base_value 
		 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = scope:firing_court_position }
				scope:employee = { has_any_court_position = yes }
			}
			add = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = aristocratic_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = populist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						global_variable_list_size = {
							name = traditionalist_senate_italy
							value > 9
						}
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
					}
					AND = {
						liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
						has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
						has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
					}
				}
				}
			}
			add = {
				value = 10000
				desc = SENATE_BRIBED_VICAR
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
					has_title = title:k_tekke
				}
			}
			add = 200 #to stop AI from revoking alot 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:liege = {
					has_relation_rival = scope:employee
				}
			}
			add = 900 # rival isn't that big of a deal
		}
	} 
}
k_trebizond_governor = { 
	skill = stewardship max_available_positions = 1 
	category = court_position_roman_vicar 
	opinion = { value = regular_court_position_opinion } 
	aptitude_level_breakpoints = { 20 40 60 80 } 
	aptitude = { value = 25 add = { value = stewardship multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_stewardship } add = { value = martial multiply = 1.25 max = 25 desc = court_position_skill_martial } if = { limit = { has_trait = administrator } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_administrator_trait } } if = { limit = { has_trait = overseer } add = { value = 20 desc = court_position_overseer_trait } } } 
	is_shown = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
		OR = {
			any_vassal = {
				has_title = title:k_trebizond
			}
			AND = {
			has_title = title:k_trebizond
			NOT = { capital_county.kingdom = title:k_trebizond  }
			}
		}
	} 
	valid_position = { 
		OR = { government_has_flag = government_is_imperial government_has_flag = government_is_imperial_cult government_has_flag = government_is_administrative }
	} 

	valid_character = { 
		scope:employee = { 
			OR = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							exists = title:k_trebizond.holder
						
							NOT = { scope:liege = title:k_trebizond.holder }
						
						}
						title:k_trebizond.holder = {
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = populist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = traditionalist_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = aristocratic_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = populist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = traditionalist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						liege = {
							has_title = title:k_trebizond
						}
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				has_title = title:k_trebizond
				
			}
		} 
	} 
	revoke_cost = { 
		prestige = {
			value = 1000
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = title:k_trebizond.holder
					title:k_trebizond.holder = {

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
							AND = {

								global_variable_list_size = {
									name = aristocratic_senate_italy
									value > 9
								}
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}

							}

								has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}
							AND = {
								liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
								has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
								has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
							}

							}

				add = {

				}
			}
		} 
	}

		poor = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.2 } 
		average = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.3 } 
		good = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.4 } 
		excellent = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.5 } 
	} 
	modifier = { monthly_prestige = minor_court_position_prestige_salary } 
	on_court_position_received = { 
		if = {
		limit = {scope:employee = { is_landed = no } }
			scope:liege = { save_scope_as = employer_saved } 
			scope:employee = { save_scope_as = employee_saved } 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { type = granted save_scope_as = title_change add_claim_on_loss = no } 
			title:k_trebizond = { change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } }

                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
                                    AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_populists_eastern
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_eastern
                                    }
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = aristocratic_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = populist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}

									}
									AND = {

										global_variable_list_size = {
											name = traditionalist_senate_italy
											value > 9
										}
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_italy
									}
									AND = {
										liege = { access_to_italian_senate = yes }
										has_character_flag = bribed_populists_italy
										has_character_flag = bribed_traditionalist_italy
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					OR = {
						liege = {
							has_title = title:k_rum
						}
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = low_senator
						has_trait = senator
						has_trait = high_senator
					}
				}
				has_title = title:k_rum
				
			}
		} 
	}

	salary = { round = no gold = medium_court_position_salary } 
	scaling_employer_modifiers = { 
		terrible = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.1 } 
		poor = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.2 } 
		average = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.3 } 
		good = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.4 } 
		excellent = { monthly_county_control_growth_add = 0.5 } 
	} 
	modifier = { monthly_prestige = minor_court_position_prestige_salary } 
	on_court_position_received = { 
		if = {
		limit = {scope:employee = { is_landed = no } }
			scope:liege = { save_scope_as = employer_saved } 
			scope:employee = { save_scope_as = employee_saved } 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { type = granted save_scope_as = title_change add_claim_on_loss = no } 
			title:k_rum = { change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } 
			title:k_rum = { random_in_de_facto_hierarchy = { limit = { tier = tier_county holder.highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy OR = { holder = { has_title = title:k_rum } holder = { highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom } } } change_title_holder_include_vassals = { holder = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } holder = { random_vassal = { limit = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_county } change_liege = { liege = scope:employee change = scope:title_change } } } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change 
			create_title_and_vassal_change = { 
				type = swear_fealty 
				save_scope_as = title_change_2 add_claim_on_loss = no 
			} 
			scope:employee_saved = { change_liege = { liege = scope:employer_saved change = scope:title_change_2 } } 
			resolve_title_and_vassal_change = scope:title_change_2 
			change_government = imperial_government
		}
	} 
	on_court_position_revoked = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes k_rum_revoked_effect = yes } 
	on_court_position_invalidated = { seneschal_title_revoked_effect = yes }
	candidate_score = { 
		value = 250 
		add = scope:base_value 
		add = court_position_candidate_score_base_value 
		 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = scope:firing_court_position }
				scope:employee = { has_any_court_position = yes }
			}
			add = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:employee = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
                                        liege = { access_to_eastern_senate = yes }
                                        global_variable_list_size = {
                                            name = aristocratic_senate_eastern
                                            value > 9
                                        }
                                        has_character_flag = bribed_aristocrats_eastern
                                    }
